**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching

4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Grafana Datasource Plugin Query Path

The query path through the Grafana codebase spans three main phases:

### 1. Query Request Handler
- **`pkg/api/ds_query.go`** — `QueryMetricsV2` is the HTTP handler for `POST /ds/query`. It binds the request body, delegates to the query service, and serializes the response. `getDSQueryEndpoint` conditionally routes to the new k8s API server path.
- **`pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`** — The new API-server-style handler (`queryREST.Connect` + `handleQuery`) used when `FlagQueryServiceRewrite` is enabled.

### 2. Plugin Backend Query Dispatch
- **`pkg/services/query/query.go`** — `ServiceImpl.queryData` orchestrates the dispatch: parses requests, handles expressions, single-datasource, or concurrent multi-datasource queries.
- **`pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`** — Defines `plugins.Client` interface.
- **`pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go`** — Concrete `Service.QueryData` that looks up the plugin in the registry and calls through (via gRPC) to the actual plugin backend.
- **`pkg/registry/apis/query/client/plugin.go`** — `pluginClient.QueryData` for the new query-service path, with access control checks and context resolution.
- Supporting files: `clientapi/clientapi.go`, `client/instance_provider.go`, `dsquerierclient/qs_datasource_client_builder.go`, `plugincontext/plugincontext.go`, `adapters/adapters.go`.

### 3. Query Response Transformation
- **`pkg/expr/transform.go`** — `Service.TransformData` runs server-side expression evaluation (math, reduce, threshold, SQL, etc.) over datasource results.
- **`pkg/expr/converter.go`** — `ResultConverter.Convert` transforms frames for expression pipelines.
- **`pkg/expr/query_convert.go`** — `ConvertB
... (truncated)

New Query API Server Handler\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`** \u2014 The Kubernetes API server-style query endpoint used by the new query service. `queryREST.Connect` handles incoming POST requests, parsing the body into `query.QueryDataRequest` and delegating to `handleQuery`. `handleQuery` marshals queries into `dtos.MetricRequest` format and calls `service.QueryData`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/register.go`** \u2014 Registers `QueryAPIBuilder`, wires up `newQueryREST`, `pluginsStorage`, expression query schemas, and the `singleTenantInstanceProvider` via `NewSingleTenantInstanceProvider`.\\n\\n## 3. instantiated via `NewSingleTenantInstanceProvider` which takes the raw `plugins.Client`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/clientapi/clientapi.go`** \u2014 Defines the `QueryDataClient` interface, `Instance` interface, and `InstanceProvider` interface used throughout the query-service path.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/dsquerierclient/qs_datasource_client_builder.go`** \u2014 `QSDatasourceClientBuilder` interface and implementations that bridge the legacy `ServiceImpl` to the new query-service client (multi-tenant or null/no-op for single-tenant). `QsDatasourceClientBuilderWithInstance` delegates to the `Instance.GetDataSourceClient`.\\n\\n**`pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/query.go`** \u2014 `PluginHandler.QueryDataHandler()`: the aggregator-side HTTP handler for plugin QueryData requests (used in the plugin aggregation API server), which dispatches directly to `h.client.QueryData` and wraps the result as `aggregationv0alpha1.QueryDataResponse`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/querier.go`** \u2014 `DefaultQuerier` wraps a `plugins.Client` to implement the `Querier` interface used in the per-datasource API server flows.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/register.go`** \u2014 Registers datasource API groups and defines the `PluginClient` interface subset (QueryData, CheckHealth, CallResource, ConversionHandler) used by datasource API servers.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/queryconvert.go`** \u2014 `queryConvertREST` handles the query-convert subresource, parsing incoming HTTP requests into `query.QueryDataRequest` format.\\n\\n## 5. Plugin Context Resolution\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/plugincontext.go`** \u2014 `Provider.GetWithDataSource` and `Provider.PluginContextForDataSource` resolve `backend.PluginContext` (including `DataSourceInstanceSettings`) from the datasource model and plugin store before dispatching queries.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/adapters/adapters.go`** \u2014 `ModelToInstanceSettings` converts a `datasources.DataSource` database model to `backend.DataSourceInstanceSettings`, decrypting secure JSON data.\\n\\n## 6. Query Response Transformation\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/transform.go`** \u2014 `Service.TransformData` runs server-side expression evaluation over datasource query results, executing math, reduce, threshold, SQL, and other expression node types to produce the final `backend.QueryDataResponse`.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/service.go`** \u2014 Defines `expr.Service` (the expression service with `TransformData`) and the `ResultConverter` field used to convert datasource frame results for expression pipelines.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/converter.go`** \u2014 `ResultConverter.Convert` transforms raw `data.Frames` from datasource query responses into formats suitable for use in expression node pipelines.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/query_convert.go`** \u2014 `ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest` bridges the `backend.QueryDataRequest` format to the k8s-style `data.QueryDataRequest` used in the multi-tenant query-service flow (called from `handleQuerySingleDatasource`).\\n\\n## 7.
